============================================================
FILE: ./Dockerfile
============================================================
FROM node:20-alpine AS build

WORKDIR /app

COPY package*.json ./

RUN npm install

COPY . .

RUN npm run build


FROM nginx:alpine

COPY --from=build /app/dist /usr/share/nginx/html

COPY nginx.conf /etc/nginx/conf.d/default.conf

EXPOSE 80

CMD ["nginx", "-g", "daemon off;"]

============================================================
FILE: ./README.md
============================================================
# lowcortisol-webapp

This template should help get you started developing with Vue 3 in Vite.

## Recommended IDE Setup

[VS Code](https://code.visualstudio.com/) + [Vue (Official)](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=Vue.volar) (and disable Vetur).

## Recommended Browser Setup

- Chromium-based browsers (Chrome, Edge, Brave, etc.):
  - [Vue.js devtools](https://chromewebstore.google.com/detail/vuejs-devtools/nhdogjmejiglipccpnnnanhbledajbpd)
  - [Turn on Custom Object Formatter in Chrome DevTools](http://bit.ly/object-formatters)
- Firefox:
  - [Vue.js devtools](https://addons.mozilla.org/en-US/firefox/addon/vue-js-devtools/)
  - [Turn on Custom Object Formatter in Firefox DevTools](https://fxdx.dev/firefox-devtools-custom-object-formatters/)

## Customize configuration

See [Vite Configuration Reference](https://vite.dev/config/).

## Project Setup

```sh
npm install
```

### Compile and Hot-Reload for Development

```sh
npm run dev
```

### Compile and Minify for Production

```sh
npm run build
```

' SHARED

package "shared" {
  package "domain" {
    abstract class BaseEntity {
      +Guid Id
      +DateTime CreatedAt
      +DateTime? UpdatedAt
      +void SetCreatedAt()
      +void SetUpdatedAt()
    }

    interface Repository<T> {
      +Task<IEnumerable<T>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task<T?> GetByIdAsync(Guid id)
      +Task AddAsync(T entity)
      +void Update(T entity)
      +void Delete(T entity)
    }

    interface UnitOfWork {
      +Task<int> CompleteAsync()
    }
  }

  package "application" {
    class ApiResponse<T> {
      +bool Success
      +string Message
      +T Data
      +IEnumerable<string> Error
    }

    class PageResult<T> {
      +IEnumerable<T> Item
      +int Page
      +int PageSize
      +int Total
    }
  }

  package "infrastructure" {
    class DateTimeProvider {
      +DateTime UtcNow()
    }

    class LowCortisolDbContext {
      +DbSet<User> User
      +DbSet<AccessProfile> AccessProfile
      +DbSet<Permission> Permission
      +DbSet<AuthSession> AuthSession
      +DbSet<Plan> Plan
      +DbSet<PlanFeature> PlanFeature
      +DbSet<Subscription> Subscription
      +DbSet<Payment> Payment
      +DbSet<ServiceRequest> ServiceRequest
      +DbSet<Workplace> Workplace
      +DbSet<Site> Site
      +DbSet<SiteMember> SiteMember
      +DbSet<SiteDeviceAssignment> SiteDeviceAssignment
      +DbSet<Device> Device
      +DbSet<Sensor> Sensor
      +DbSet<Valve> Valve
      +DbSet<DeviceCommand> DeviceCommand
      +DbSet<MonitoringSession> MonitoringSession
      +DbSet<Reading> Reading
      +DbSet<Anomaly> Anomaly
      +DbSet<Report> Report
      +DbSet<Alert> Alert
      +DbSet<Threshold> Threshold
      +DbSet<Incident> Incident
      +DbSet<NotificationChannel> NotificationChannel
      +DbSet<AlertDelivery> AlertDelivery
      +DbSet<SupportTicket> SupportTicket
      +DbSet<SupportMessage> SupportMessage
      +DbSet<SupportAgent> SupportAgent
      +DbSet<SupportConversation> SupportConversation
      +DbSet<KnowledgeArticle> KnowledgeArticle
      +Task<int> SaveChangesAsync()
    }

    class EfUnitOfWork {
      -LowCortisolDbContext context
      +Task<int> CompleteAsync()
    }
  }
}

' IAM

package "iam" {
  package "domain" {
    class User {
      +Guid Id
      +string FullName
      +string Email
      +string Phone
      +string PasswordHash
      +string Status
      +Guid AccessProfileId
      +void Activate()
      +void Deactivate()
      +void UpdateProfile(string fullName, string phone)
    }

    class AccessProfile {
      +Guid Id
      +string Name
      +string Role
      +ICollection<Permission> Permission
      +bool HasPermission(string code)
    }

    class Permission {
      +Guid Id
      +string Code
      +string Description
    }

    class AuthSession {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid UserId
      +string Token
      +string RefreshToken
      +bool IsActive
      +DateTime ExpiresAt
      +void Revoke()
      +bool IsExpired()
    }

    interface UserRepository {
      +Task<User?> FindByEmailAsync(string email)
      +Task<User?> FindByIdAsync(Guid id)
      +Task AddAsync(User user)
      +void Update(User user)
    }

    interface AccessProfileRepository {
      +Task<AccessProfile?> FindByIdAsync(Guid id)
      +Task<AccessProfile?> FindDefaultOwnerProfileAsync()
    }

    interface AuthSessionRepository {
      +Task AddAsync(AuthSession session)
      +Task<AuthSession?> FindActiveByTokenAsync(string token)
      +void Update(AuthSession session)
    }
  }

  package "application" {
    class SignInCommand {
      +string Email
      +string Password
    }

    class SignUpCommand {
      +string FullName
      +string Email
      +string Phone
      +string Password
    }

    class RecoverPasswordCommand {
      +string Email
    }

    class UpdateProfileCommand {
      +Guid UserId
      +string FullName
      +string Phone
    }

    class UserDto {
      +Guid Id
      +string FullName
      +string Email
      +string Phone
      +string Status
      +Guid AccessProfileId
    }

    class AccessProfileDto {
      +Guid Id
      +string Name
      +string Role
      +IEnumerable<string> Permission
    }

    class AuthSessionDto {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid UserId
      +string Token
      +bool IsActive
      +DateTime ExpiresAt
    }

    class AuthResult {
      +UserDto User
      +AccessProfileDto AccessProfile
      +AuthSessionDto AuthSession
    }

    class AuthApplicationService {
      -UserRepository userRepository
      -AccessProfileRepository accessProfileRepository
      -AuthSessionRepository authSessionRepository
      -PasswordHashingService passwordHashingService
      -TokenService tokenService
      -UnitOfWork unitOfWork
      +Task<AuthResult> SignInAsync(SignInCommand command)
      +Task<AuthResult> SignUpAsync(SignUpCommand command)
      +Task RecoverPasswordAsync(RecoverPasswordCommand command)
      +Task SignOutAsync(string token)
    }

    class UserApplicationService {
      -UserRepository userRepository
      -UnitOfWork unitOfWork
      +Task<UserDto> GetProfileAsync(Guid userId)
      +Task<UserDto> UpdateProfileAsync(UpdateProfileCommand command)
    }
  }

  package "infrastructure" {
    interface PasswordHashingService {
      +string Hash(string password)
      +bool Verify(string password, string hash)
    }

    interface TokenService {
      +string GenerateToken(User user)
      +string GenerateRefreshToken()
    }

    class BcryptPasswordHashingService
    class JwtTokenService
    class EfUserRepository
    class EfAccessProfileRepository
    class EfAuthSessionRepository
  }

  package "interface" {
    class AuthController {
      +Task<IActionResult> SignIn(SignInCommand command)
      +Task<IActionResult> SignUp(SignUpCommand command)
      +Task<IActionResult> RecoverPassword(RecoverPasswordCommand command)
      +Task<IActionResult> SignOut()
    }

    class UserController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetProfile()
      +Task<IActionResult> UpdateProfile(UpdateProfileCommand command)
    }

    class AccessProfileController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetCurrentProfile()
    }
  }
}

package "plan" {
  package "domain" {
    class Plan {
      +Guid Id
      +string Name
      +string Code
      +string Description
      +decimal Price
      +string Currency
      +string BillingPeriod
      +int MaxSite
      +int MaxDevice
      +bool Recommended
      +ICollection<PlanFeature> Feature
      +void AddFeature(PlanFeature feature)
    }

    class PlanFeature {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid PlanId
      +string Name
      +string Description
      +bool Included
    }

    class Subscription {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid UserId
      +Guid WorkplaceId
      +Guid PlanId
      +string Status
      +DateTime StartedAt
      +DateTime? ExpiresAt
      +bool AutoRenew
      +void Activate()
      +void Cancel()
      +void ChangePlan(Guid newPlanId)
    }

    class Payment {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SubscriptionId
      +decimal Amount
      +string Currency
      +string Method
      +string Status
      +DateTime? PaidAt
      +void MarkAsPaid()
      +void MarkAsFailed()
    }

    class ServiceRequest {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SubscriptionId
      +string Type
      +string Description
      +string Status
      +void Resolve()
      +void Close()
    }

    class SubscriptionPolicyService {
      +bool CanChangePlan(Subscription subscription)
      +bool CanCancel(Subscription subscription)
      +bool RequiresPayment(Plan plan)
    }

    interface PlanRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Plan>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task<Plan?> GetByIdAsync(Guid id)
    }

    interface SubscriptionRepository {
      +Task<Subscription?> FindActiveByUserIdAsync(Guid userId)
      +Task<IEnumerable<Subscription>> FindByUserIdAsync(Guid userId)
      +Task AddAsync(Subscription subscription)
      +void Update(Subscription subscription)
    }

    interface PaymentRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Payment>> FindBySubscriptionIdAsync(Guid subscriptionId)
      +Task AddAsync(Payment payment)
    }

    interface ServiceRequestRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<ServiceRequest>> FindBySubscriptionIdAsync(Guid subscriptionId)
      +Task AddAsync(ServiceRequest request)
    }
  }

  package "application" {
    class SubscribeCommand {
      +Guid UserId
      +Guid WorkplaceId
      +Guid PlanId
      +string PaymentMethod
    }

    class ChangePlanCommand {
      +Guid UserId
      +Guid NewPlanId
    }

    class CancelSubscriptionCommand {
      +Guid UserId
      +string Reason
    }

    class PlanDto {
      +Guid Id
      +string Name
      +string Code
      +decimal Price
      +string Currency
      +int MaxSite
      +int MaxDevice
      +bool Recommended
      +IEnumerable<PlanFeatureDto> Feature
    }

    class PlanFeatureDto {
      +Guid Id
      +string Name
      +string Description
      +bool Included
    }

    class SubscriptionDto {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid UserId
      +Guid WorkplaceId
      +Guid PlanId
      +string Status
      +bool AutoRenew
    }

    class PaymentDto {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SubscriptionId
      +decimal Amount
      +string Currency
      +string Method
      +string Status
      +DateTime? PaidAt
    }

    class ServiceRequestDto {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SubscriptionId
      +string Type
      +string Description
      +string Status
    }

    class PlanSummaryDto {
      +int TotalPlan
      +string ActivePlanName
      +string SubscriptionStatus
      +decimal TotalPaid
      +int MaxSite
      +int MaxDevice
    }

    class PlanApplicationService {
      -PlanRepository planRepository
      -SubscriptionRepository subscriptionRepository
      -PaymentRepository paymentRepository
      -ServiceRequestRepository serviceRequestRepository
      -SubscriptionPolicyService subscriptionPolicyService
      -UnitOfWork unitOfWork
      +Task<IEnumerable<PlanDto>> GetPlanAsync()
      +Task<PlanDto> GetPlanByIdAsync(Guid id)
      +Task<SubscriptionDto?> GetActiveSubscriptionAsync(Guid userId)
      +Task<SubscriptionDto> SubscribeAsync(SubscribeCommand command)
      +Task<SubscriptionDto> ChangePlanAsync(ChangePlanCommand command)
      +Task<SubscriptionDto> CancelSubscriptionAsync(CancelSubscriptionCommand command)
      +Task<PlanSummaryDto> GetSummaryAsync(Guid userId)
    }
  }

  package "infrastructure" {
    class EfPlanRepository
    class EfSubscriptionRepository
    class EfPaymentRepository
    class EfServiceRequestRepository
  }

  package "interface" {
    class PlanController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetPlan()
      +Task<IActionResult> GetPlanById(Guid id)
    }

    class SubscriptionController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetActive()
      +Task<IActionResult> Subscribe(SubscribeCommand command)
      +Task<IActionResult> ChangePlan(ChangePlanCommand command)
      +Task<IActionResult> Cancel(CancelSubscriptionCommand command)
    }

    class PaymentController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetPayment()
    }
  }
}

package "workplace" {
  package "domain" {
    class Workplace {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid OwnerId
      +string Name
      +string Description
      +ICollection<Site> Site
      +void Rename(string name)
    }

    class Site {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid WorkplaceId
      +string Name
      +string Address
      +string Type
      +string Status
      +decimal WaterConsumption
      +decimal GasConsumption
      +int ActiveSensor
      +int ActiveIncident
      +void Activate()
      +void SetMaintenance()
      +void UpdateConsumption(decimal water, decimal gas)
    }

    class SiteMember {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SiteId
      +Guid UserId
      +string FullName
      +string Email
      +string Role
      +void ChangeRole(string role)
    }

    class SiteDeviceAssignment {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SiteId
      +Guid DeviceId
      +string DeviceName
      +string DeviceType
      +string Status
      +void Activate()
      +void Deactivate()
    }

    interface WorkplaceRepository {
      +Task<Workplace?> FindByOwnerIdAsync(Guid ownerId)
      +Task<Workplace?> FindByIdAsync(Guid id)
      +Task AddAsync(Workplace workplace)
      +void Update(Workplace workplace)
    }

    interface SiteRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Site>> FindByWorkplaceIdAsync(Guid workplaceId)
      +Task<Site?> FindByIdAsync(Guid siteId)
      +Task AddAsync(Site site)
      +void Update(Site site)
      +void Delete(Site site)
    }

    interface SiteMemberRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<SiteMember>> FindBySiteIdAsync(Guid siteId)
      +Task AddAsync(SiteMember member)
    }

    interface SiteDeviceAssignmentRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<SiteDeviceAssignment>> FindBySiteIdAsync(Guid siteId)
      +Task AddAsync(SiteDeviceAssignment assignment)
    }
  }

  package "application" {
    class CreateSiteCommand {
      +Guid WorkplaceId
      +string Name
      +string Address
      +string Type
    }

    class AssignMemberToSiteCommand {
      +Guid SiteId
      +Guid UserId
      +string FullName
      +string Email
      +string Role
    }

    class AssignDeviceToSiteCommand {
      +Guid SiteId
      +Guid DeviceId
      +string DeviceName
      +string DeviceType
    }

    class WorkplaceDto {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid OwnerId
      +string Name
      +string Description
    }

    class SiteDto {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid WorkplaceId
      +string Name
      +string Address
      +string Type
      +string Status
      +decimal WaterConsumption
      +decimal GasConsumption
      +int ActiveSensor
      +int ActiveIncident
    }

    class SiteMemberDto {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SiteId
      +Guid UserId
      +string FullName
      +string Email
      +string Role
    }

    class SiteDeviceAssignmentDto {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SiteId
      +Guid DeviceId
      +string DeviceName
      +string DeviceType
      +string Status
    }

    class WorkplaceSummaryDto {
      +int TotalSite
      +int ActiveSite
      +int MaintenanceSite
      +int TotalMember
      +int TotalDeviceAssignment
      +decimal WaterConsumption
      +decimal GasConsumption
    }

    class WorkplaceApplicationService {
      -WorkplaceRepository workplaceRepository
      -SiteRepository siteRepository
      -SiteMemberRepository siteMemberRepository
      -SiteDeviceAssignmentRepository siteDeviceAssignmentRepository
      -UnitOfWork unitOfWork
      +Task<WorkplaceDto?> GetWorkplaceAsync(Guid ownerId)
      +Task<IEnumerable<SiteDto>> GetSiteAsync(Guid workplaceId, string type)
      +Task<SiteDto> CreateSiteAsync(CreateSiteCommand command)
      +Task AssignMemberToSiteAsync(AssignMemberToSiteCommand command)
      +Task AssignDeviceToSiteAsync(AssignDeviceToSiteCommand command)
      +Task<WorkplaceSummaryDto> GetSummaryAsync(Guid workplaceId)
    }
  }

  package "infrastructure" {
    class EfWorkplaceRepository
    class EfSiteRepository
    class EfSiteMemberRepository
    class EfSiteDeviceAssignmentRepository
  }

  package "interface" {
    class WorkplaceController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetCurrentWorkplace()
      +Task<IActionResult> GetSummary()
    }

    class SiteController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetSite(string type)
      +Task<IActionResult> GetSiteById(Guid id)
      +Task<IActionResult> CreateSite(CreateSiteCommand command)
      +Task<IActionResult> DeleteSite(Guid id)
    }

    class SiteMemberController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetMemberBySite(Guid siteId)
      +Task<IActionResult> AssignMember(AssignMemberToSiteCommand command)
    }

    class SiteDeviceAssignmentController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetAssignmentBySite(Guid siteId)
      +Task<IActionResult> AssignDevice(AssignDeviceToSiteCommand command)
    }
  }
}

package "device-control" {
  package "domain" {
    class Device {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Name
      +string Type
      +string Status
      +ICollection<Sensor> Sensor
      +ICollection<Valve> Valve
      +ICollection<DeviceCommand> Command
      +bool IsOnline()
      +void SetOnline()
      +void SetOffline()
    }

    class Sensor {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid DeviceId
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Name
      +string ResourceType
      +decimal CurrentValue
      +string Unit
      +decimal Threshold
      +string Status
      +bool HasExceededThreshold()
      +void UpdateReading(decimal value)
    }

    class Valve {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid DeviceId
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Name
      +string ResourceType
      +string Status
      +int OpeningPercentage
      +void Open()
      +void Close()
    }

    class DeviceCommand {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid DeviceId
      +string CommandType
      +string Status
      +void MarkExecuted()
      +void MarkFailed()
    }

    interface DeviceRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Device>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task<Device?> FindByIdAsync(Guid id)
      +Task<IEnumerable<Device>> FindBySiteIdAsync(Guid siteId)
      +Task AddAsync(Device device)
      +void Update(Device device)
    }

    interface SensorRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Sensor>> FindByDeviceIdAsync(Guid deviceId)
      +Task AddAsync(Sensor sensor)
      +void Update(Sensor sensor)
    }

    interface ValveRepository {
      +Task<Valve?> FindByIdAsync(Guid id)
      +Task<IEnumerable<Valve>> FindByDeviceIdAsync(Guid deviceId)
      +void Update(Valve valve)
    }

    interface DeviceCommandRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<DeviceCommand>> FindByDeviceIdAsync(Guid deviceId)
      +Task AddAsync(DeviceCommand command)
    }
  }

  package "application" {
    class CreateDeviceCommand {
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Name
      +string Type
    }

    class LinkSensorCommand {
      +Guid DeviceId
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Name
      +string ResourceType
      +string Unit
      +decimal Threshold
    }

    class ExecuteDeviceCommand {
      +Guid DeviceId
      +string CommandType
    }

    class DeviceDto {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Name
      +string Type
      +string Status
      +IEnumerable<SensorDto> Sensor
      +IEnumerable<ValveDto> Valve
      +IEnumerable<DeviceCommandDto> Command
    }

    class SensorDto {
      +Guid Id
      +string Name
      +string ResourceType
      +decimal CurrentValue
      +string Unit
      +decimal Threshold
      +bool HasExceededThreshold
    }

    class ValveDto {
      +Guid Id
      +string Name
      +string ResourceType
      +string Status
      +int OpeningPercentage
      +bool IsOpen
    }

    class DeviceCommandDto {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid DeviceId
      +string CommandType
      +string Status
    }

    class DeviceControlSummaryDto {
      +int TotalDevice
      +int ActiveSensor
      +int ClosedValve
      +int TotalSensor
      +int TotalValve
      +int TotalCommand
    }

    class DeviceControlApplicationService {
      -DeviceRepository deviceRepository
      -SensorRepository sensorRepository
      -ValveRepository valveRepository
      -DeviceCommandRepository commandRepository
      -UnitOfWork unitOfWork
      +Task<IEnumerable<DeviceDto>> GetDeviceAsync()
      +Task<DeviceDto> CreateDeviceAsync(CreateDeviceCommand command)
      +Task<SensorDto> LinkSensorAsync(LinkSensorCommand command)
      +Task<ValveDto> OpenValveAsync(Guid valveId)
      +Task<ValveDto> CloseValveAsync(Guid valveId)
      +Task<DeviceCommandDto> ExecuteCommandAsync(ExecuteDeviceCommand command)
      +Task<DeviceControlSummaryDto> GetSummaryAsync()
    }
  }

  package "infrastructure" {
    class EfDeviceRepository
    class EfSensorRepository
    class EfValveRepository
    class EfDeviceCommandRepository
  }

  package "interface" {
    class DeviceController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetDevice()
      +Task<IActionResult> CreateDevice(CreateDeviceCommand command)
    }

    class SensorController {
      +Task<IActionResult> LinkSensor(LinkSensorCommand command)
    }

    class ValveController {
      +Task<IActionResult> OpenValve(Guid id)
      +Task<IActionResult> CloseValve(Guid id)
    }

    class DeviceCommandController {
      +Task<IActionResult> ExecuteCommand(ExecuteDeviceCommand command)
      +Task<IActionResult> GetCommand(Guid deviceId)
    }
  }
}

' MONITORING

package "monitoring" {
  package "domain" {
    class MonitoringSession {
      +Guid Id
      +bool IsActive
      +int TotalReading
      +int TotalAnomaly
      +DateTime StartedAt
      +DateTime? FinishedAt
      +void AddReading()
      +void AddAnomaly()
      +void Finish()
    }

    class Reading {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid MonitoringSessionId
      +Guid SensorId
      +Guid SiteId
      +string ResourceType
      +decimal Value
      +string Unit
      +string Status
      +DateTime MeasuredAt
      +bool IsCritical()
    }

    class Anomaly {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid ReadingId
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Severity
      +string Description
      +string Status
      +void Resolve()
      +void Close()
    }

    class Report {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Period
      +decimal TotalWater
      +decimal TotalGas
      +int AnomalyCount
      +DateTime GeneratedAt
    }

    class AnomalyDetectionService {
      +Anomaly? DetectFromReading(Reading reading)
    }

    interface MonitoringSessionRepository {
      +Task<MonitoringSession?> FindActiveAsync()
      +Task AddAsync(MonitoringSession session)
      +void Update(MonitoringSession session)
    }

    interface ReadingRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Reading>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task AddAsync(Reading reading)
    }

    interface AnomalyRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Anomaly>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task AddAsync(Anomaly anomaly)
    }

    interface ReportRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Report>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task AddAsync(Report report)
    }
  }

  package "application" {
    class CreateReadingCommand {
      +Guid SensorId
      +Guid SiteId
      +string ResourceType
      +decimal Value
      +string Unit
    }

    class CreateReportCommand {
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Period
    }

    class MonitoringSummaryDto {
      +decimal TotalWater
      +decimal TotalGas
      +int CriticalAnomaly
    }

    class MonitoringApplicationService {
      -MonitoringSessionRepository monitoringSessionRepository
      -ReadingRepository readingRepository
      -AnomalyRepository anomalyRepository
      -ReportRepository reportRepository
      -AnomalyDetectionService anomalyDetectionService
      -UnitOfWork unitOfWork
      +Task<MonitoringSummaryDto> GetSummaryAsync()
      +Task<MonitoringSession> GetActiveSessionAsync()
      +Task<IEnumerable<Reading>> GetReadingAsync()
      +Task<Reading> CreateReadingAsync(CreateReadingCommand command)
      +Task<IEnumerable<Anomaly>> GetAnomalyAsync()
      +Task<Report> CreateReportAsync(CreateReportCommand command)
    }
  }

  package "infrastructure" {
    class EfMonitoringSessionRepository
    class EfReadingRepository
    class EfAnomalyRepository
    class EfReportRepository
  }

  package "interface" {
    class MonitoringController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetSummary()
      +Task<IActionResult> GetActiveSession()
    }

    class ReadingController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetReading()
      +Task<IActionResult> CreateReading(CreateReadingCommand command)
    }

    class ReportController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetReport()
      +Task<IActionResult> CreateReport(CreateReportCommand command)
    }
  }
}

package "notification" {
  package "domain" {
    class Alert {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SiteId
      +Guid SensorId
      +string ResourceType
      +string Title
      +string Description
      +string Severity
      +string Status
      +void Resolve()
      +void Close()
    }

    class Threshold {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid SiteId
      +Guid SensorId
      +string ResourceType
      +decimal WarningLimit
      +decimal CriticalLimit
      +string Unit
      +bool Enabled
      +void Enable()
      +void Disable()
    }

    class Incident {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid AlertId
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Title
      +string Description
      +string Priority
      +string Status
      +Guid? AssignedTo
      +void AssignTo(Guid userId)
      +void Resolve()
      +void Close()
    }

    class NotificationChannel {
      +Guid Id
      +string Name
      +string Type
      +string Destination
      +bool Enabled
      +void Enable()
      +void Disable()
    }

    class AlertDelivery {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid AlertId
      +Guid ChannelId
      +string Status
      +DateTime? SentAt
      +void MarkSent()
      +void MarkFailed()
    }

    class AlertPolicyService {
      +Incident? CreateIncidentIfRequired(Alert alert)
    }

    interface AlertRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Alert>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task<Alert?> FindByIdAsync(Guid id)
      +Task AddAsync(Alert alert)
      +void Update(Alert alert)
    }

    interface ThresholdRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Threshold>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task AddAsync(Threshold threshold)
    }

    interface IncidentRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<Incident>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task AddAsync(Incident incident)
      +void Update(Incident incident)
    }

    interface NotificationChannelRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<NotificationChannel>> GetEnabledAsync()
    }

    interface AlertDeliveryRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<AlertDelivery>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task AddAsync(AlertDelivery delivery)
    }
  }

  package "application" {
    class CreateAlertCommand {
      +Guid SiteId
      +Guid SensorId
      +string ResourceType
      +string Title
      +string Description
      +string Severity
    }

    class CreateThresholdCommand {
      +Guid SiteId
      +Guid SensorId
      +string ResourceType
      +decimal WarningLimit
      +decimal CriticalLimit
      +string Unit
    }

    class NotificationSummaryDto {
      +int TotalAlert
      +int CriticalAlert
      +int OpenIncident
      +int ActiveThreshold
      +int ChannelEnabled
      +int DeliverySent
    }

    class NotificationApplicationService {
      -AlertRepository alertRepository
      -ThresholdRepository thresholdRepository
      -IncidentRepository incidentRepository
      -NotificationChannelRepository notificationChannelRepository
      -AlertDeliveryRepository alertDeliveryRepository
      -AlertPolicyService alertPolicyService
      -UnitOfWork unitOfWork
      +Task<IEnumerable<Alert>> GetAlertAsync()
      +Task<Alert> CreateAlertAsync(CreateAlertCommand command)
      +Task<Alert> ResolveAlertAsync(Guid alertId)
      +Task<Alert> CloseAlertAsync(Guid alertId)
      +Task<Threshold> CreateThresholdAsync(CreateThresholdCommand command)
      +Task<IEnumerable<AlertDelivery>> SendAlertAsync(Guid alertId)
      +Task<NotificationSummaryDto> GetSummaryAsync()
    }
  }

  package "infrastructure" {
    class EfAlertRepository
    class EfThresholdRepository
    class EfIncidentRepository
    class EfNotificationChannelRepository
    class EfAlertDeliveryRepository
  }

  package "interface" {
    class AlertController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetAlert()
      +Task<IActionResult> CreateAlert(CreateAlertCommand command)
      +Task<IActionResult> ResolveAlert(Guid id)
      +Task<IActionResult> CloseAlert(Guid id)
      +Task<IActionResult> SendAlert(Guid id)
    }

    class ThresholdController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetThreshold()
      +Task<IActionResult> CreateThreshold(CreateThresholdCommand command)
    }

    class IncidentController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetIncident()
    }
  }
}

package "support" {
  package "domain" {
    class SupportTicket {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid UserId
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Title
      +string Description
      +string Category
      +string Priority
      +string Status
      +Guid? AssignedAgentId
      +void AssignTo(Guid agentId)
      +void Resolve()
      +void Close()
    }

    class SupportMessage {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid TicketId
      +Guid SenderId
      +string SenderType
      +string Content
      +string Status
      +void MarkAsRead()
    }

    class SupportAgent {
      +Guid Id
      +string FullName
      +string Email
      +string Specialty
      +string Status
      +void SetAvailable()
      +void SetBusy()
    }

    class SupportConversation {
      +Guid Id
      +Guid TicketId
      +string Status
      +void Close()
    }

    class KnowledgeArticle {
      +Guid Id
      +string Title
      +string Summary
      +string Category
      +string Content
      +int HelpfulCount
      +void MarkHelpful()
    }

    class SupportPriorityService {
      +string ResolvePriority(string category)
      +bool ShouldAssignImmediately(SupportTicket ticket)
    }

    interface SupportTicketRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<SupportTicket>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task<SupportTicket?> FindByIdAsync(Guid id)
      +Task AddAsync(SupportTicket ticket)
      +void Update(SupportTicket ticket)
    }

    interface SupportMessageRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<SupportMessage>> FindByTicketIdAsync(Guid ticketId)
      +Task AddAsync(SupportMessage message)
    }

    interface SupportAgentRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<SupportAgent>> GetAllAsync()
      +Task<SupportAgent?> FindAvailableBySpecialtyAsync(string specialty)
      +void Update(SupportAgent agent)
    }

    interface KnowledgeArticleRepository {
      +Task<IEnumerable<KnowledgeArticle>> GetAllAsync()
    }
  }

  package "application" {
    class CreateSupportTicketCommand {
      +Guid UserId
      +Guid SiteId
      +string Title
      +string Description
      +string Category
    }

    class SendSupportMessageCommand {
      +Guid TicketId
      +Guid SenderId
      +string SenderType
      +string Content
    }

    class SupportSummaryDto {
      +int TotalTicket
      +int OpenTicket
      +int AssignedTicket
      +int ResolvedTicket
      +int AvailableAgent
      +int TotalArticle
    }

    class SupportApplicationService {
      -SupportTicketRepository supportTicketRepository
      -SupportMessageRepository supportMessageRepository
      -SupportAgentRepository supportAgentRepository
      -KnowledgeArticleRepository knowledgeArticleRepository
      -SupportPriorityService supportPriorityService
      -UnitOfWork unitOfWork
      +Task<IEnumerable<SupportTicket>> GetTicketAsync()
      +Task<SupportTicket> CreateTicketAsync(CreateSupportTicketCommand command)
      +Task<SupportTicket> ResolveTicketAsync(Guid ticketId)
      +Task<SupportTicket> CloseTicketAsync(Guid ticketId)
      +Task<SupportMessage> SendMessageAsync(SendSupportMessageCommand command)
      +Task<IEnumerable<SupportAgent>> GetAgentAsync()
      +Task<IEnumerable<KnowledgeArticle>> GetArticleAsync()
      +Task<SupportSummaryDto> GetSummaryAsync()
    }
  }

  package "infrastructure" {
    class EfSupportTicketRepository
    class EfSupportMessageRepository
    class EfSupportAgentRepository
    class EfKnowledgeArticleRepository
  }

  package "interface" {
    class SupportTicketController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetTicket()
      +Task<IActionResult> CreateTicket(CreateSupportTicketCommand command)
      +Task<IActionResult> ResolveTicket(Guid id)
      +Task<IActionResult> CloseTicket(Guid id)
    }

    class SupportMessageController {
      +Task<IActionResult> SendMessage(SendSupportMessageCommand command)
    }

    class KnowledgeArticleController {
      +Task<IActionResult> GetArticle()
    }
  }

note bottom
Backend real proyectado para C#:
ASP.NET Core Web API + Entity Framework Core.
Las clases se mantienen en singular porque cada una representa
una entidad, servicio, repositorio, controller o caso de uso individual.
Los endpoints REST pueden permanecer en plural porque representan colecciones.
end note

============================================================
FILE: ./docs/database-diagram.puml
============================================================
@startuml
title LowCortisol Platform - Database Diagram

skinparam linetype ortho
skinparam shadowing false
skinparam packageStyle rectangle

skinparam entity {
  BackgroundColor #FFFFFF
  BorderColor #1F2937
  ArrowColor #1F2937
}

' ==========================================================
' IAM
' ==========================================================

entity "user" as user {
  * id : uuid <<PK>>
  --
  full_name : varchar
  email : varchar <<unique>>
  phone : varchar
  password_hash : varchar
  status : varchar
  access_profile_id : uuid <<FK>>
  created_at : datetime
  updated_at : datetime
}

entity "access_profile" as access_profile {
  * id : uuid <<PK>>
  --
  name : varchar
  role : varchar
  created_at : datetime
  updated_at : datetime
}

entity "permission" as permission {
  * id : uuid <<PK>>
  --
  code : varchar <<unique>>
  description : varchar
  created_at : datetime
  updated_at : datetime
}

entity "access_profile_permission" as access_profile_permission {
  * id : uuid <<PK>>
  --
  access_profile_id : uuid <<FK>>
  permission_id : uuid <<FK>>
  created_at : datetime
  updated_at : datetime
}

entity "auth_session" as auth_session {
  * id : uuid <<PK>>
  --

access_profile ||--o{ user : "access_profile_id"

permission ||--o{ access_profile_permission : "permission_id"
user ||--o{ auth_session : "user_id"

user ||--o{ workplace : "owner_id"
workplace ||--o{ site : "workplace_id"

user ||--o{ subscription : "user_id"
workplace ||--o{ subscription : "workplace_id"
plan ||--o{ subscription : "plan_id"
plan ||--o{ plan_feature : "plan_id"
subscription ||--o{ payment : "subscription_id"
subscription ||--o{ service_request : "subscription_id"

site ||--o{ site_member : "site_id"
user ||--o{ site_member : "user_id"

site ||--o{ device : "site_id"
site ||--o{ site_device_assignment : "site_id"
device ||--o{ site_device_assignment : "device_id"

device ||--o{ sensor : "device_id"
device ||--o{ valve : "device_id"
device ||--o{ device_command : "device_id"

site ||--o{ sensor : "site_id"
site ||--o{ valve : "site_id"

monitoring_session ||--o{ reading : "monitoring_session_id"
sensor ||--o{ reading : "sensor_id"
site ||--o{ reading : "site_id"

reading ||--o| anomaly : "reading_id"
site ||--o{ anomaly : "site_id"
site ||--o{ report : "site_id"

site ||--o{ alert : "site_id"
sensor ||--o{ alert : "sensor_id"

site ||--o{ threshold : "site_id"
sensor ||--o{ threshold : "sensor_id"

alert ||--o{ incident : "alert_id"
site ||--o{ incident : "site_id"
user ||--o{ incident : "assigned_to"

alert ||--o{ alert_delivery : "alert_id"
notification_channel ||--o{ alert_delivery : "channel_id"

user ||--o{ support_ticket : "user_id"
site ||--o{ support_ticket : "site_id"
support_agent ||--o{ support_ticket : "assigned_agent_id"

support_ticket ||--o{ support_message : "ticket_id"
support_ticket ||--o| support_conversation : "ticket_id"

package "Shared" {

  class AppRoute {
    +path: string
    +name: string
    +component: Component
    +meta: object
  }

  class ApiClientService {
    +baseUrl: string
    +get(endpoint: string, params?: object): Promise
    +post(endpoint: string, payload: object): Promise
    +patch(endpoint: string, payload: object): Promise
    +delete(endpoint: string): Promise
  }

  class AuthSessionService {
    +getCurrentUser(): User
    +getCurrentUserId(): string
    +saveSession(session: AuthSession): void
    +clearSession(): void
    +hasSession(): boolean
  }

  class TranslationService {
    +currentLanguage: string
    +loadLanguage(language: string): Promise
    +t(key: string): string
    +setLanguage(language: string): void
  }

  class SubscriptionAccessService {
    +hasActiveSubscription(userId: string): Promise<boolean>
    +canAccessProtectedRoute(userId: string): Promise<boolean>
  }

  class UiCardComponent {
    +title: string
    +render(): void
  }

  class LanguageSwitcherComponent {
    +selectedLanguage: string
    +changeLanguage(language: string): void
  }

  class AppLayoutComponent {
    +showNavigation: boolean
    +render(): void
  }

  class RouteGuard {
    +beforeEach(to: AppRoute): boolean
    +requiresAuth(route: AppRoute): boolean
    +requiresSubscription(route: AppRoute): boolean
  }
}

package "IAM" {

  class User {
    +id: string
    +fullName: string
    +email: string
    +phone: string
    +password: string
    +status: string
    +accessProfileId: string
  }

  class AccessProfile {
    +id: string
    +name: string
    +role: string
    +permissions: string[]
  }

  class AuthSession {
    +id: string
    +userId: string
    +token: string
    +status: string
    +createdAt: string
  }

  class IamStore {
    +state: object
    +signIn(email: string, password: string): Promise
    +signUp(payload: object): Promise
    +recoverPassword(email: string): Promise
    +updateProfile(payload: object): Promise
    +signOut(): void
    +restoreSession(): void
  }

  class IamFacade {
    -iamApiService: IamApiService
    +signIn(email: string, password: string): Promise
    +signUp(payload: object): Promise
    +recoverPassword(email: string): Promise
    +getProfile(userId: string): Promise
    +updateProfile(userId: string, payload: object): Promise
    +signOut(): void
  }

  class IamApiService {
    +getUser(): Promise<User[]>
    +getUserByEmail(email: string): Promise<User>
    +createUser(payload: object): Promise<User>
    +updateUser(userId: string, payload: object): Promise<User>
    +getAccessProfile(profileId: string): Promise<AccessProfile>
    +createSession(payload: object): Promise<AuthSession>
    +getSession(userId: string): Promise<AuthSession>
    +closeSession(sessionId: string): Promise
  }

  class LoginPageComponent {
    +email: string
    +password: string
    +submit(): Promise
  }

  class RegisterPageComponent {
    +fullName: string
    +email: string
    +phone: string
    +password: string
    +submit(): Promise
  }

  class RecoverPageComponent {
    +email: string
    +submit(): Promise
  }

  class ProfilePageComponent {
    +user: User
    +accessProfile: AccessProfile
    +session: AuthSession
    +updateProfile(): Promise
    +signOut(): void
  }
}

package "Plan" {

  class Plan {
    +id: string

    +deviceLimit: number
    +recommended: boolean

    +cancelledAt: string

    +id: string

    +status: string
    +paidAt: string
  }

  class ServiceRequest {
    +id: string

    +cancelSubscription(): Promise
    +loadPayment(): Promise
    +loadServiceRequest(): Promise
  }

  class PlanFacade {

    +getSubscription(): Promise

    +getServiceRequest(): Promise

    +cancelSubscription(subscriptionId: string): Promise
    +getSummary(): Promise
  }

  class PlanApiService {

    +message: string
    +createdAt: string
  }

  class SupportAgent {
    +id: string
    +fullName: string
    +email: string
    +status: string
  }

  class SupportConversation {
    +id: string
    +ticketId: string
    +status: string
  }

  class KnowledgeArticle {
    +id: string
    +title: string
    +category: string
    +content: string
    +usefulCount: number
  }

  class SupportStore {
    +state: object
    +loadSupport(): Promise
    +selectTicket(ticketId: string): void
    +createTicket(payload: object): Promise
    +sendMessage(payload: object): Promise
    +resolveTicket(ticketId: string): Promise
    +closeTicket(ticketId: string): Promise
  }

  class SupportFacade {
    -supportApiService: SupportApiService
    +getTicket(): Promise
    +getMessage(ticketId: string): Promise
    +getAgent(): Promise
    +getConversation(): Promise
    +getKnowledgeArticle(): Promise
    +createTicket(payload: object): Promise
    +sendMessage(payload: object): Promise
    +resolveTicket(ticketId: string): Promise
    +closeTicket(ticketId: string): Promise
  }

  class SupportApiService {
    +getTicket(): Promise<SupportTicket[]>
    +getMessage(ticketId: string): Promise<SupportMessage[]>
    +getAgent(): Promise<SupportAgent[]>
    +getConversation(): Promise<SupportConversation[]>
    +getKnowledgeArticle(): Promise<KnowledgeArticle[]>
    +createTicket(payload: object): Promise<SupportTicket>
    +sendMessage(payload: object): Promise<SupportMessage>
    +resolveTicket(ticketId: string): Promise<SupportTicket>
    +closeTicket(ticketId: string): Promise<SupportTicket>
    +getSummary(): Promise<object>
  }

  class SupportPageComponent {
    +selectedTicket: SupportTicket
    +message: string
    +loadSupport(): Promise
    +selectTicket(ticketId: string): void
    +createTicket(): Promise
    +sendMessage(): Promise
    +resolveTicket(ticketId: string): Promise
    +closeTicket(ticketId: string): Promise
  }
}

@startuml
title LowCortisol Platform - Workplace Context - Backend Component Diagram

!define C4Puml https://raw.githubusercontent.com/plantuml-stdlib/C4-PlantUML/master

Container_Boundary(workplaceContext, "Workplace Bounded Context") {

  Component(interfaceLayer, "Interface Layer", "ASP.NET Core Controllers", "Exposes workplace, site, site member, and site device assignment endpoints through WorkplaceController, SiteController, SiteMemberController, and SiteDeviceAssignmentController.")
@startuml
title LowCortisol Platform - Workspace Backend Component Diagram

!define C4Puml https://raw.githubusercontent.com/plantuml-stdlib/C4-PlantUML/master
!includeurl C4Puml/C4_Component.puml

LAYOUT_WITH_LEGEND()

Container(spa, "Single Page Application", "Vue / Vite", "Consumes workspace backend endpoints.")
ContainerDb(database, "Database", "SQL Server / PostgreSQL", "Stores workspaces, sites, members, and device assignments.")

Container_Boundary(workspace, "Workspace") {

  Component(interface, "Interface", "ASP.NET Core Controllers", "Exposes workspace, site, member, and assignment endpoints through WorkspaceController, SiteController, SiteMemberController, and SiteDeviceAssignmentController.")

  Component(application, "Application", "Application Services / Commands / DTOs", "Coordinates workspace retrieval, site creation, site filtering, member assignment, device assignment, and summary generation.")

  Component(domain, "Domain", "Domain Model / Business Rules", "Contains Workspace, Site, SiteMember, SiteDeviceAssignment, and workspace business rules.")

  Component(infrastructure, "Infrastructure", "Repositories / Persistence Services", "Implements repositories and database access for workspaces, sites, members, and assignments.")
}

Rel(spa, interface, "Consumes workspace endpoints", "HTTPS/JSON")

Rel(interface, application, "Delegates commands and queries")
Rel(application, domain, "Applies workspace business rules")
Rel(application, infrastructure, "Uses repositories and persistence services")

Rel(infrastructure, database, "Reads and writes workspace data", "EF Core")

@enduml
  Component(applicationLayer, "Application Layer", "Application Services / Commands / DTOs", "Coordinates workplace use cases such as getting the current workplace, creating sites, filtering sites, assigning members, assigning devices, and generating workplace summaries.")

  Component(domainLayer, "Domain Layer", "Domain Model / Business Rules", "Contains Workplace, Site, SiteMember, SiteDeviceAssignment, and workplace management business rules.")

  Component(infrastructureLayer, "Infrastructure Layer", "Repositories / Persistence Services", "Implements repositories and database access for workplaces, sites, site members, and site device assignments.")

  Component(subscriptionAccessPolicy, "Subscription Access Policy", "Domain Service", "Validates whether the current subscription allows creating more sites or assigning more devices.")

  Component(workplaceSummaryService, "Workplace Summary Service", "Domain/Application Service", "Calculates workplace metrics such as total sites, active sites, maintenance sites, members, assignments, and resource consumption.")
}

Rel(spa, interfaceLayer, "Consumes workplace endpoints", "HTTPS/JSON")

Rel(interfaceLayer, applicationLayer, "Delegates commands and queries")
Rel(applicationLayer, domainLayer, "Applies workplace business rules")
Rel(applicationLayer, infrastructureLayer, "Uses repositories and persistence services")

Rel(applicationLayer, subscriptionAccessPolicy, "Validates plan limits")
Rel(applicationLayer, workplaceSummaryService, "Calculates workplace summary")

Rel(infrastructureLayer, database, "Reads and writes workplace context data", "EF Core")

@enduml

server {
    listen 80;
    server_name _;

    root /usr/share/nginx/html;
    index index.html;

    location / {
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
    }

    error_page 404 /index.html;
}

FILE: ./src/app/device-control/application/dto/create-device.dto.js
============================================================
export class CreateDeviceDto {
    constructor({
                    siteId = "",
                    name = "",
                    type = "hub",
                    status = "online",
                } = {}) {
        this.siteId = siteId;
        this.name = name.trim();
        this.type = type;
        this.status = status;
    }

    isValid() {
        return Boolean(this.siteId && this.name && this.type);
    }

    toPayload() {
        return {
            siteId: this.siteId,
            name: this.name,
            type: this.type,
            status: this.status,
        };
    }
}

export class ExecuteDeviceCommandDto {
    constructor({
                    deviceId = "",
                    commandType = "sync",
                    payload = {},
                } = {}) {
        this.deviceId = deviceId;
        this.commandType = commandType;
        this.payload = payload;
    }

    isValid() {
        return Boolean(this.deviceId && this.commandType);
    }

    toPayload() {
        return {
            deviceId: this.deviceId,
            commandType: this.commandType,
            payload: this.payload,
        };
    }
}

export class LinkSensorDto {
    constructor({
                    deviceId = "",
                    siteId = "",
                    name = "",
                    resourceType = "water",
                    unit = "L",
                    threshold = 100,
                } = {}) {
        this.deviceId = deviceId;
        this.siteId = siteId;
        this.name = name.trim();
        this.resourceType = resourceType;
        this.unit = unit;
        this.threshold = threshold;
    }

    isValid() {
        return Boolean(this.deviceId && this.siteId && this.name && this.resourceType);
    }

    toPayload() {
        return {
            deviceId: this.deviceId,
            siteId: this.siteId,
            name: this.name,
            resourceType: this.resourceType,
            unit: this.unit,
            threshold: this.threshold,
        };
    }
}

    constructor({
                    valveId = "",
                    status = "closed",
                    openingPercentage = 0,
                } = {}) {
        this.valveId = valveId;
        this.status = status;
        this.openingPercentage = openingPercentage;
    }

    isValid() {
        return Boolean(this.valveId && this.status);
    }

    toPayload() {
        return {
            valveId: this.valveId,
            status: this.status,
            openingPercentage: this.openingPercentage,
        };
    }
}

import { DeviceControlApiService } from "../../infrastructure/api/device-control-api.service";

export class DeviceControlFacade {
    constructor() {
        this.deviceControlApiService = new DeviceControlApiService();
    }

    async getDevices() {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.getDevices();
    }

    async getDeviceById(deviceId) {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.getDeviceById(deviceId);
    }

    async getDevicesBySite(siteId) {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.getDevicesBySite(siteId);
    }

    async createDevice(payload) {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.createDevice(payload);
    }

    async getSensors() {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.getSensors();
    }

    async linkSensor(payload) {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.linkSensor(payload);
    }

    async getValves() {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.getValves();
    }

    async updateValveStatus(payload) {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.updateValveStatus(payload);
    }

    async executeCommand(payload) {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.executeCommand(payload);
    }

    async getCommands() {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.getCommands();
    }

    async getSummary() {
        return this.deviceControlApiService.getSummary();
    }
}

FILE: ./src/app/device-control/application/store/device-control.store.js
============================================================
import { reactive, readonly } from "vue";
import { DeviceControlFacade } from "../services/device-control.facade";

const deviceControlFacade = new DeviceControlFacade();

const state = reactive({
    devices: [],
    sensors: [],
    valves: [],
    commands: [],
    summary: {
        totalDevices: 0,
        onlineDevices: 0,
        totalSensors: 0,
        activeSensors: 0,
        totalValves: 0,
        openValves: 0,
        closedValves: 0,
        commandsExecuted: 0,
    },
    selectedDeviceId: null,
    loading: false,
    error: null,
    message: "",
});

async function loadDevicePage() {
    state.loading = true;
    state.error = null;

    try {
        state.devices = await deviceControlFacade.getDevices();
        state.sensors = await deviceControlFacade.getSensors();
        state.valves = await deviceControlFacade.getValves();
        state.commands = await deviceControlFacade.getCommands();
        state.summary = await deviceControlFacade.getSummary();

        if (!state.selectedDeviceId && state.devices.length > 0) {
            state.selectedDeviceId = state.devices[0].id;
        }
    } catch (error) {
        state.error = error.message || "No se pudo cargar la gestión de dispositivos.";
    } finally {
        state.loading = false;
    }
}

function selectDevice(deviceId) {
    state.selectedDeviceId = deviceId;
}

function getSelectedDevice() {
    return state.devices.find((device) => device.id === state.selectedDeviceId) ?? null;
}

async function createDevice(payload) {
    const device = await deviceControlFacade.createDevice(payload);

    await loadDevicePage();

    state.selectedDeviceId = device.id;
    state.message = "Dispositivo creado correctamente.";

    return device;
}

async function linkSensor(payload) {
    const sensor = await deviceControlFacade.linkSensor(payload);

    await loadDevicePage();

    state.message = "Sensor vinculado correctamente.";

    return sensor;
}

async function closeValve(valveId) {
    const valve = await deviceControlFacade.updateValveStatus({
        valveId,
        status: "closed",
        openingPercentage: 0,
    });

    await loadDevicePage();

    state.message = "Válvula cerrada correctamente.";

    return valve;
}

async function openValve(valveId) {
    const valve = await deviceControlFacade.updateValveStatus({
        valveId,
        status: "open",
        openingPercentage: 100,
    });

    await loadDevicePage();

    state.message = "Válvula abierta correctamente.";

    return valve;
}

async function executeSyncCommand(deviceId) {
    const command = await deviceControlFacade.executeCommand({
        deviceId,
        commandType: "sync",
        payload: {
            source: "devices-page",
        },
    });

    await loadDevicePage();

    state.message = "Comando ejecutado correctamente.";

    return command;
}

export function useDeviceControlStore() {
    return {
        state: readonly(state),
        loadDevicePage,
        selectDevice,
        getSelectedDevice,
        createDevice,
        linkSensor,
        closeValve,
        openValve,
        executeSyncCommand,
    };
}

FILE: ./src/app/device-control/domain/model/device-assignment.entity.js
============================================================
import { BaseEntity } from "../../../shared/domain/model/base.entity";

export class DeviceAssignment extends BaseEntity {
    constructor({
                    id = null,
                    deviceId = "",
                    siteId = "",
                    assignedAt = new Date(),
                    status = "linked",
                    createdAt = null,
                    updatedAt = null,
                } = {}) {
        super({ id, createdAt, updatedAt });

        this.deviceId = deviceId;
        this.siteId = siteId;
        this.assignedAt = assignedAt ? new Date(assignedAt) : new Date();
        this.status = status;
    }

    unlink() {
        this.status = "unlinked";
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    relink() {
        this.status = "linked";
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    get isLinked() {
        return this.status === "linked";
    }
}

FILE: ./src/app/device-control/domain/model/device-command.entity.js
============================================================
import { BaseEntity } from "../../../shared/domain/model/base.entity";

export class DeviceCommand extends BaseEntity {
    constructor({
                    id = null,
                    deviceId = "",
                    commandType = "sync",
                    payload = {},
                    status = "pending",
                    executedAt = null,
                    createdAt = null,
                    updatedAt = null,
                } = {}) {
        super({ id, createdAt, updatedAt });

        this.deviceId = deviceId;
        this.commandType = commandType;
        this.payload = payload;
        this.status = status;
        this.executedAt = executedAt ? new Date(executedAt) : null;
    }

    markAsExecuted() {
        this.status = "executed";
        this.executedAt = new Date();
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    markAsFailed() {
        this.status = "failed";
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    get statusLabel() {
        const labels = {
            pending: "Pendiente",
            executed: "Ejecutado",
            failed: "Fallido",
        };

        return labels[this.status] ?? "Sin estado";
    }

    get commandLabel() {
        const labels = {
            sync: "Sincronizar",
            closeValve: "Cerrar válvula",
            openValve: "Abrir válvula",
            reboot: "Reiniciar",
        };

        return labels[this.commandType] ?? "Comando";
    }
}

FILE: ./src/app/device-control/domain/model/device.entity.js
============================================================
import { BaseEntity } from "../../../shared/domain/model/base.entity";

export class Device extends BaseEntity {
    constructor({
                    id = null,
                    siteId = "",
                    name = "",
                    type = "hub",
                    status = "online",
                    sensors = [],
                    valves = [],
                    commands = [],
                    createdAt = null,
                    updatedAt = null,
                } = {}) {
        super({ id, createdAt, updatedAt });

        this.siteId = siteId;
        this.name = name;
        this.type = type;
        this.status = status;
        this.sensors = sensors;
        this.valves = valves;
        this.commands = commands;
    }

    addSensor(sensor) {
        this.sensors.push(sensor);
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    addValve(valve) {
        this.valves.push(valve);
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    registerCommand(command) {
        this.commands.push(command);
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    setOnline() {
        this.status = "online";
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    setOffline() {
        this.status = "offline";
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    get isOnline() {
        return this.status === "online";
    }

    get typeLabel() {
        const labels = {
            hub: "Hub",
            sensor: "Sensor",
            valve: "Válvula",
        };

        return labels[this.type] ?? "Dispositivo";
    }

    get statusLabel() {
        const labels = {
            online: "En línea",
            offline: "Desconectado",
            maintenance: "Mantenimiento",
        };

        return labels[this.status] ?? "Sin estado";
    }
}

FILE: ./src/app/device-control/domain/model/sensor.entity.js
============================================================
import { BaseEntity } from "../../../shared/domain/model/base.entity";

export class Sensor extends BaseEntity {
    constructor({
                    id = null,
                    deviceId = "",
                    siteId = "",
                    name = "",
                    resourceType = "water",
                    status = "active",
                    currentValue = 0,
                    unit = "L",
                    threshold = 100,
                    createdAt = null,
                    updatedAt = null,
                } = {}) {
        super({ id, createdAt, updatedAt });

        this.deviceId = deviceId;
        this.siteId = siteId;
        this.name = name;
        this.resourceType = resourceType;
        this.status = status;
        this.currentValue = currentValue;
        this.unit = unit;
        this.threshold = threshold;
    }

    updateReading(value) {
        this.currentValue = value;
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    deactivate() {
        this.status = "inactive";
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    activate() {
        this.status = "active";
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    get isActive() {
        return this.status === "active";
    }

    get hasExceededThreshold() {
        return Number(this.currentValue) >= Number(this.threshold);
    }

    get resourceLabel() {
        const labels = {
            water: "Agua",
            gas: "Gas",
        };

        return labels[this.resourceType] ?? "Recurso";
    }
}

============================================================
FILE: ./src/app/device-control/domain/model/valve.entity.js
============================================================
import { BaseEntity } from "../../../shared/domain/model/base.entity";

export class Valve extends BaseEntity {
    constructor({
                    id = null,
                    deviceId = "",
                    siteId = "",
                    name = "",
                    resourceType = "gas",
                    status = "open",
                    openingPercentage = 100,
                    createdAt = null,
                    updatedAt = null,
                } = {}) {
        super({ id, createdAt, updatedAt });

        this.deviceId = deviceId;
        this.siteId = siteId;
        this.name = name;
        this.resourceType = resourceType;
        this.status = status;
        this.openingPercentage = openingPercentage;
    }

    open() {
        this.status = "open";
        this.openingPercentage = 100;
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    close() {
        this.status = "closed";
        this.openingPercentage = 0;
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    setOpeningPercentage(value) {
        const percentage = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Number(value)));

        this.openingPercentage = percentage;
        this.status = percentage === 0 ? "closed" : "open";
        this.updateTimestamp();
    }

    get isOpen() {
        return this.status === "open";
    }

    get resourceLabel() {
        const labels = {
            water: "Agua",
            gas: "Gas",
        };

        return labels[this.resourceType] ?? "Recurso";
    }

    get statusLabel() {
        const labels = {
            open: "Abierta",
            closed: "Cerrada",
            maintenance: "Mantenimiento",
        };

        return labels[this.status] ?? "Sin estado";
    }
}

============================================================
FILE: ./src/app/device-control/domain/services/device-status-policy.service.js
============================================================
export class DeviceStatusPolicyService {
    static canExecuteCommand(device) {
        return device?.status === "online";
    }

    static canCloseValve(valve) {
        return valve?.status === "open";
    }

    static canOpenValve(valve) {
        return valve?.status === "closed";
    }

    static getSensorHealth(sensor) {
        if (!sensor.isActive) return "inactive";
        if (sensor.hasExceededThreshold) return "critical";

        return "normal";
    }
}

import { BaseApiEndpoint } from "../../../shared/infrastructure/api/base-api.endpoint";
import { DeviceAssembler } from "../assembler/device.assembler";

export class DeviceApiEndpoint extends BaseApiEndpoint {
    constructor() {
        super("/devices", new DeviceAssembler());
    }

    async getDevicesBySite(siteId) {
        const response = await this.getFromPath(`?siteId=${siteId}`);
        const resource = response?.data ?? response ?? [];

        return this.assembler.toEntities(resource);
    }

    async executeCommand(deviceId, resource) {
        return this.postToPath(`/${deviceId}/commands`, resource);
    }
}

============================================================
FILE: ./src/app/device-control/infrastructure/api/device-control-api.service.js
============================================================
import { ApiClientService } from "../../../shared/infrastructure/http/api-client.service";

function normalizeDevice(device, sensors = [], valves = [], commands = []) {
    return {
        ...device,
        isOnline: device.status === "online",
        sensors: sensors.filter((sensor) => sensor.deviceId === device.id),
        valves: valves
            .filter((valve) => valve.deviceId === device.id)
            .map(normalizeValve),
        commands: commands.filter((command) => command.deviceId === device.id),
    };
}

function normalizeValve(valve) {
    return {
        ...valve,
        isOpen: valve.status === "open",
    };
}

function normalizeSensor(sensor) {
    return {
        ...sensor,
        hasExceededThreshold: Boolean(sensor.hasExceededThreshold),
    };
}

export class DeviceControlApiService {
    async getDevices() {
        const [devices, sensors, valves, commands] = await Promise.all([
            this.getRawDevices(),
            this.getSensors(),
            this.getValves(),
            this.getCommands(),
        ]);

        return devices.map((device) =>
            normalizeDevice(device, sensors, valves, commands)
        );
    }

    async getDevice() {
        return this.getDevices();
    }

    async getRawDevices() {
        return ApiClientService.get("/devices");
    }

    async getSensors() {
        const sensors = await ApiClientService.get("/sensors");
        return sensors.map(normalizeSensor);
    }

    async getValves() {
        const valves = await ApiClientService.get("/valves");
        return valves.map(normalizeValve);
    }

    async getCommands() {
        return ApiClientService.get("/commands");
    }

    async createDevice(payload) {
        return ApiClientService.post("/devices", {
            siteId: payload.siteId || "SITE-001",
            name: payload.name,
            type: payload.type || "hub",
            status: payload.status || "online",
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        });
    }

    async linkSensor(payload) {
        const sensor = {
            deviceId: payload.deviceId,
            siteId: payload.siteId,
            name: payload.name,
            resourceType: payload.resourceType || "water",
            currentValue: Number(payload.currentValue || 0),
            unit: payload.unit || "L",
            threshold: Number(payload.threshold || 300),
            status: "active",
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        };

        sensor.hasExceededThreshold = sensor.currentValue > sensor.threshold;

        return ApiClientService.post("/sensors", sensor);
    }

    async closeValve(valveId) {
        return ApiClientService.patch(`/valves/${valveId}`, {
            status: "closed",
            openingPercentage: 0,
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        });
    }

    async openValve(valveId) {
        return ApiClientService.patch(`/valves/${valveId}`, {
            status: "open",
            openingPercentage: 100,
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        });
    }

    async executeSyncCommand(deviceId) {
        return ApiClientService.post("/commands", {
            deviceId,
            commandType: "sync",
            status: "executed",
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        });
    }

    async getSummary() {
        const [devices, sensors, valves, commands] = await Promise.all([
            this.getRawDevices(),
            this.getSensors(),
            this.getValves(),
            this.getCommands(),
        ]);

        return {
            totalDevices: devices.length,
            activeSensors: sensors.filter((sensor) => sensor.status === "active").length,
            closedValves: valves.filter((valve) => valve.status === "closed").length,
            totalSensors: sensors.length,
            totalValves: valves.length,
            totalCommands: commands.length,
        };
    }
}

FILE: ./src/app/device-control/infrastructure/assembler/device.assembler.js
============================================================
import { BaseAssembler } from "../../../shared/infrastructure/assembler/base.assembler";
import { Device } from "../../domain/model/device.entity";
import { DeviceResource } from "../resource/device.resource";

import { SensorAssembler } from "./sensor.assembler";
import { ValveAssembler } from "./valve.assembler";
import { DeviceCommandAssembler } from "./device-command.assembler";

export class DeviceAssembler extends BaseAssembler {
    constructor() {
        super();

        this.sensorAssembler = new SensorAssembler();
        this.valveAssembler = new ValveAssembler();
        this.deviceCommandAssembler = new DeviceCommandAssembler();
    }

    toEntity(resource) {
        return new Device({
            id: resource.id,
            siteId: resource.siteId,
            name: resource.name,
            type: resource.type,
            status: resource.status,
            sensors: this.sensorAssembler.toEntities(resource.sensors ?? []),
            valves: this.valveAssembler.toEntities(resource.valves ?? []),
            commands: this.deviceCommandAssembler.toEntities(resource.commands ?? []),
            createdAt: resource.createdAt,
            updatedAt: resource.updatedAt,
        });
    }

    toResource(entity) {
        return new DeviceResource({
            id: entity.id,
            siteId: entity.siteId,
            name: entity.name,
            type: entity.type,
            status: entity.status,
            sensors: this.sensorAssembler.toResource(entity.sensors ?? []),
            valves: this.valveAssembler.toResource(entity.valves ?? []),
            commands: this.deviceCommandAssembler.toResource(entity.commands ?? []),
            createdAt: entity.createdAt,
            updatedAt: entity.updatedAt,
        });
    }
}

<template>
  <button
      type="button"
      class="device-card"
      :class="{ 'device-card--active': active }"
  >
    <div>
      <h3>{{ device.name }}</h3>
      <p>{{ getDeviceTypeLabel(device.type) }} · {{ device.siteId }}</p>
    </div>

    <span class="badge" :class="device.isOnline ? 'badge-success' : 'badge-warning'">
      {{ getStatusLabel(device.status) }}
    </span>
  </button>
</template>

<script setup>
import { useTranslation } from "../../../../shared/application/services/translation.service";

defineProps({
  device: {
    type: Object,
    required: true,
  },
  active: {
    type: Boolean,
    default: false,
  },
});

const { t } = useTranslation();

function getDeviceTypeLabel(type) {
  const keys = {
    hub: "deviceControl.types.hub",
    sensor: "deviceControl.types.sensor",
    valve: "deviceControl.types.valve",
  };

  return t(keys[type] ?? "deviceControl.types.device");
}

function getStatusLabel(status) {
  const keys = {
    online: "deviceControl.status.online",
    offline: "deviceControl.status.offline",
    maintenance: "deviceControl.status.maintenance",
  };

  return t(keys[status] ?? "deviceControl.status.unknown");
}
</script>

<template>
  <article class="valve-control">
    <div>
      <h3>{{ valve.name }}</h3>
      <p>{{ getResourceLabel(valve.resourceType) }} · {{ valve.openingPercentage }}%</p>
    </div>

    <div class="valve-control__actions">
      <span class="badge" :class="valve.isOpen ? 'badge-success' : 'badge-danger'">
        {{ getStatusLabel(valve.status) }}
      </span>

      <button
          v-if="valve.isOpen"
          class="btn-secondary"
          type="button"
          @click="$emit('close', valve.id)"
      >
        {{ t('deviceControl.actions.close') }}
      </button>

      <button
          v-else
          class="btn-secondary"
          type="button"
          @click="$emit('open', valve.id)"
      >
        {{ t('deviceControl.actions.open') }}
      </button>
    </div>
  </article>
</template>

<script setup>
import { useTranslation } from "../../../../shared/application/services/translation.service";

defineProps({
  valve: {
    type: Object,
    required: true,
  },
});

defineEmits(["close", "open"]);

const { t } = useTranslation();

function getResourceLabel(resourceType) {
  const keys = {
    water: "deviceControl.resource.water",
    gas: "deviceControl.resource.gas",
  };

  return t(keys[resourceType] ?? "deviceControl.resource.water");
}

function getStatusLabel(status) {
  const keys = {
    open: "deviceControl.status.open",
    closed: "deviceControl.status.closed",
    maintenance: "deviceControl.status.maintenance",
  };

  return t(keys[status] ?? "deviceControl.status.unknown");
}
</script>

<template>
  <AppLayout>
    <section class="page-header">
      <div>
        <h1 class="page-title">
          {{ t('deviceControl.devices.title') }}

      </UiCard>

        <p class="summary-number">{{ state.summary.activeSensors }}</p>

              <p>{{ getDeviceTypeLabel(selectedDevice.type) }} · {{ selectedDevice.siteId }}</p>

              {{ getStatusLabel(selectedDevice.status) }}
            </span>

              <strong>{{ selectedDevice.sensors.length }}</strong>
            </div>

              <span>{{ t('deviceControl.devices.availableValves') }}</span>
              <strong>{{ selectedDevice.valves.length }}</strong>
            </div>

            <div class="metric-row">
              <span>{{ t('deviceControl.devices.executedCommands') }}</span>
              <strong>{{ selectedDevice.commands.length }}</strong>
            </div>
          </div>

          <button class="btn-secondary full-button" type="button" @click="handleExecuteCommand">
            {{ t('deviceControl.devices.syncDevice') }}
          </button>
        </div>

        <div v-else class="empty-state">
          {{ t('deviceControl.devices.selectDevice') }}
        </div>
      </UiCard>
    </section>

    <section class="grid grid-2 devices-bottom">
      <UiCard :title="t('deviceControl.devices.linkedSensors')">

          {{ t('deviceControl.devices.noSensors') }}

<script setup>
import { computed, onMounted } from "vue";

import AppLayout from "../../../../shared/presentation/components/app-layout/app-layout.component.vue";
import UiCard from "../../../../shared/presentation/components/ui-card/ui-card.component.vue";

import DeviceCard from "../../components/device-card/device-card.component.vue";
import SensorCard from "../../components/sensor-card/sensor-card.component.vue";
import ValveControl from "../../components/valve-control/valve-control.component.vue";

import { useDeviceControlStore } from "../../../application/store/device-control.store";
import { useTranslation } from "../../../../shared/application/services/translation.service";

const {
  state,
  loadDevicePage,
  selectDevice,
  getSelectedDevice,
  createDevice,
  linkSensor,
  closeValve,
  openValve,
  executeSyncCommand,
} = useDeviceControlStore();

const { t } = useTranslation();

const selectedDevice = computed(() => getSelectedDevice());

const selectedDeviceSensors = computed(() => selectedDevice.value?.sensors ?? []);
const selectedDeviceValves = computed(() => selectedDevice.value?.valves ?? []);

onMounted(async () => {
  await loadDevicePage();
});

async function handleCreateDevice() {
  const nextNumber = state.summary.totalDevices + 1;

  await createDevice({
    siteId: "SITE-001",
    name: `${t('deviceControl.devices.additionalHub')} ${nextNumber}`,
    type: "hub",
    status: "online",
  });
}

async function handleLinkSensor() {
  if (!selectedDevice.value) return;

  const nextNumber = state.summary.totalSensors + 1;
  const isGas = nextNumber % 2 === 0;

  await linkSensor({
    deviceId: selectedDevice.value.id,
    siteId: selectedDevice.value.siteId,
    name: `${t('deviceControl.devices.linkedSensor')} ${nextNumber}`,
    resourceType: isGas ? "gas" : "water",
    unit: isGas ? "m³" : "L",
    threshold: isGas ? 120 : 300,
  });
}

async function handleExecuteCommand() {
  if (!selectedDevice.value) return;

  await executeSyncCommand(selectedDevice.value.id);
}

function getDeviceTypeLabel(type) {
  const keys = {
    hub: "deviceControl.types.hub",
    sensor: "deviceControl.types.sensor",
    valve: "deviceControl.types.valve",
  };

  return t(keys[type] ?? "deviceControl.types.device");
}

function getStatusLabel(status) {
  const keys = {
    online: "deviceControl.status.online",
    offline: "deviceControl.status.offline",
    maintenance: "deviceControl.status.maintenance",
  };

  return t(keys[status] ?? "deviceControl.status.unknown");
}

function getCommandLabel(commandType) {
  const keys = {
    sync: "deviceControl.commands.sync",
    closeValve: "deviceControl.commands.closeValve",
    openValve: "deviceControl.commands.openValve",
    reboot: "deviceControl.commands.reboot",
  };

  return t(keys[commandType] ?? "deviceControl.commands.command");
}

function getCommandStatusLabel(status) {
  const keys = {
    pending: "deviceControl.commands.pending",
    executed: "deviceControl.commands.executed",
    failed: "deviceControl.commands.failed",
  };

  return t(keys[status] ?? "deviceControl.commands.pending");
}
</script>

export class RecoverPasswordDto {
    constructor({ email = "" } = {}) {
        this.email = email.trim().toLowerCase();
    }

    isValid() {
        return Boolean(this.email);
    }

    toPayload() {
        return {
            email: this.email,
        };
    }
}

FILE: ./src/app/iam/application/dto/sign-in.dto.js

export class SignInDto {
    constructor({ email = "", password = "" } = {}) {
        this.email = email.trim().toLowerCase();
        this.password = password;
    }

    isValid() {
        return Boolean(this.email && this.password);
    }

    toPayload() {
        return {
            email: this.email,
            password: this.password,
        };
    }
}

============================================================
FILE: ./src/app/iam/application/dto/sign-up.dto.js
============================================================
export class SignUpDto {
    constructor({
                    fullName = "",
                    email = "",
                    phone = "",
                    password = "",
                } = {}) {
        this.fullName = fullName.trim();
        this.email = email.trim().toLowerCase();
        this.phone = phone.trim();
        this.password = password;
    }

    isValid() {
        return Boolean(this.fullName && this.email && this.password);
    }

    toPayload() {
        return {
            fullName: this.fullName,
            email: this.email,
            phone: this.phone,
            password: this.password,
        };
    }
}

FILE: ./src/app/iam/application/services/iam.facade.js
